<!---->
          <h2 class="core-section-container__title section-title">
            Hakkımızda
          </h2>

<!---->
      <div class="core-section-container__content break-words">
        

          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              Hitit is a provider of new generation airline, airport and travel industry software solutions and services that support the most complicated and demanding needs of fast-growing industry players. Hitit’s brand “Crane” offers a comprehensive suite that covers the entire operational life-circle, starting from schedule and crew planning through core passenger service and ground-handling needs all the way to industrial-standard accounting and reporting tools. Crane also offers complementing solutions such as loyalty, customer management, multiple sales and distribution channels. Over 70.000 travel agencies use Hitit’s system and more than 50 billion flight queries are processed each year. Hitit’s systems produced more than 65 million passenger bookings with full GDS integration in all leading distribution systems. Hitit was awarded as “Best for Aviation Business IT Solutions Eastern Europe” and “The International Niche Technology Company of the Year”  by global award contests.
          </p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Hitit and Pakistan’s national carrier, <a class="link" href="https://pk.linkedin.com/company/pakistan-international-airlines?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Pakistan International Airlines</a> (PIA), have deepened their long-standing partnership, established in 2018 and renewed in 2023, with the implementation of Hitit’s advanced Crane Crew solution. From 1 October, PIA will transfer the management of its approximately 2,000 flight personnel to Hitit’s platform.

Featuring modules for irregular operations management (IROPS), training, and workforce planning, the solution allows the national carrier to optimise all crew planning processes and enhance operational efficiency. Fully compliant with international regulations, Crane Crew’s “Crew in Touch” mobile application strengthens communication between crew members and the operations centre, maximising crew satisfaction.

For further details, please see the full press release here.

<a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/dR_-jrPm?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/dR_-jrPm</a>

✈️

Hitit ve Pakistan'ın ulusal havayolu Pakistan International Airlines (PIA), 2018'den beri süregelen ve 2023'te yenilenen güçlü ortaklıklarını, Hitit'in gelişmiş Crane Crew (Ekip Yönetimi) çözümüyle genişletti. PIA, 1 Ekim'den itibaren yaklaşık 2000 kişilik uçuş personelinin yönetimini Hitit'in teknolojisine devrediyor. 
 
Düzensiz operasyon yönetimi (IROPS), eğitim modülü, iş gücü planlama gibi işlevsel modüllerle geliştirilen ürün sayesinde Pakistan'ın bayrak taşıyıcısı tüm ekip planlama süreçleri optimize ederek, operasyonel verimliliğini artıracak. Uluslararası düzenlemelere tam uyum sağlayan Crane Crew’un "Crew in Touch" mobil uygulaması sayesinde ekipler ile operasyon merkezi arasındaki iletişim güçlenerek uçuş ekiplerinin memnuniyetini en üst seviyeye taşıyacak. 
 
Detaylı bilgi için basın bülteninin tamamına buradan ulaşabilirsiniz.

<a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/dqdNV75U?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/dqdNV75U</a>

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fcrewmanagement&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#CrewManagement</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Faviation&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Aviation</a></p>

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">“Rackets Up” Named a Finalist at the <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/company/isildayanlar?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Işıldayanlar</a> Awards 2025 – Cast Your Vote! 

Hitit, in collaboration with the Turkish Table Tennis Federation (TMTF), has seen “Rackets Up” selected as one of 26 finalists at the Işıldayanlar Awards 2025. As Türkiye’s first and only sustainable social responsibility initiative in table tennis, the project has been recognized for its commitment to gender equality and ability to generate lasting social impact. 
  
With a presence in 411 schools, involving 430 teachers and reaching more than 160,000 children,  “Rackets Up” continues to expand its footprint nationwide. Public voting, audited by PwC Türkiye, is now open via the IŞILDAYANLAR platform, and we invite your valued support in this next stage of our journey. 

<a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/dA4t6jxQ?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/dA4t6jxQ</a>

🏓🏆

Uçan Raketler, Işıldayanlar Ödülleri 2025’te Finalde: Desteklerinizi Bekliyoruz!  

Hitit ve Türkiye Masa Tenisi Federasyonu (TMTF) iş birliğiyle yürütülen Türkiye’nin masa tenisi alanındaki ilk ve tek sürdürülebilir sosyal sorumluluk projesi olan Uçan Raketler, toplumsal cinsiyet eşitliği odağında sürdürülebilir etki yaratan projeleri görünür kılan Işıldayanlar Ödülleri’nde finale kalan 26 projeden biri oldu.  
 
Bugün 411 okulda, 430 öğretmenle ve 160 binden fazla çocukla büyüyen Uçan Raketler’i IŞILDAYANLAR platformu üzerinden PwC Türkiye denetiminde halk oylamasına sunulacak link üzerinden destekleyebilir ve bu yolculukta bizlere eşlik edebilirsiniz. 

<a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/dA4t6jxQ?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/dA4t6jxQ</a></p>

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">This year, we are delighted to join our stakeholders in marking World Tourism Day, celebrated under the theme “Tourism and Sustainable Transformation.”
 
We believe that technology will help the sustainable future of the travel industry. Guided by this vision, we support our partners in running smarter, evermore efficient operations, whilest encouraging our wider community to adopt sustainable practices. Through our innovations, we will continue working to lead the industry towards a greener, more sustainable future.

✈️🌿

Bu sene "Turizm ve Sürdürülebilir Dönüşüm” teması ile kutlanan Dünya Turizm Günü'nü tüm paydaşlarımızla birlikte kutluyoruz. 
 
Seyahat endüstrisinin sürdürülebilir geleceğinin teknolojiyle şekilleneceğine inanıyor, bu vizyonla Partnerlerimizin daha akıllı ve verimli operasyonlar yürütmesini sağlıyor, paydaşlarımızı da sürdürülebilir üretime teşvik ediyoruz. Geliştirdiğimiz inovasyonlarla sektörü daha yeşil ve sürdürülebilir bir geleceğe taşımak için çalışmaya devam edeceğiz.  

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fworldtourismday&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#WorldTourismDay</a></p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Global Success from Hitit and Pegasus: The World’s Most Comprehensive Live Airline Retail Implementation
 
Hitit and <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/company/pegasus-airlines?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Pegasus Airlines</a> have achieved a remarkable global milestone with Hitit Oxygen, the most comprehensive solution platform ever implemented in the airline retail sector. Pegasus now offers complementary travel products that enrich the passenger experience through indirect – as well as direct – sales channels.
 
This innovation not only elevates the passenger journey but also serves as an inspiration for the digital transformation of the global aviation industry.
 
You can explore the joint case study highlighting the benefits of Hitit Oxygen for Pegasus, as well as the press release featuring insights from Hitit CEO <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/nevra-onursal-karaagac-742168?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Nevra Onursal Karaagac</a> and Pegasus CEO <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/g%C3%BCliz-%C3%B6zt%C3%BCrk-7b590031?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Güliz Öztürk</a>, via the link.
 
<a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/dBiSpqF8?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/dBiSpqF8</a>
 
✈️📝
 
Hitit ve Pegasus’tan Küresel Başarı: Dünyanın En Kapsamlı Modern Havayolu Perakendeciliği Uygulaması Hayata Geçti 

Hitit ve Pegasus, havayolu perakendeciliği alanında bugüne kadar hayata geçirilen en kapsamlı çözüm platformu Hitit Oxygen ile küresel ölçekte önemli bir başarıya imza attı. Hitit Oxygen sayesinde Pegasus, yolcu deneyimini zenginleştiren tamamlayıcı seyahat ürünlerini artık endirekt satış kanalları üzerinden de sunmaya başladı. Bu yenilik, yalnızca yolcu deneyimini ileriye taşımakla kalmıyor, aynı zamanda küresel havacılık endüstrisinin dijital dönüşümüne de ilham veriyor. 

Hitit Genel Müdürü Nevra Onursal Karaağaç ve Pegasus Genel Müdürü Güliz Öztürk’ün görüşlerinin yer aldığı basın bülteni ile Hitit Oxygen’in Pegasus’a sağladığı faydaların detaylı şekilde aktarıldığı ortak vaka çalışmasına linkten ulaşabilirsiniz. 

<a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/dKFDY7Kn?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/dKFDY7Kn</a>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">A New Breath for Pegasus with Hitit Oxygen

Today, from 15:45 to 16:00 (UTC+1) at T2RL Engage 2025 – Grand Hall – Track One, join us for a compelling keynote session where <a class="link" href="https://nl.linkedin.com/in/araskubilay?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Sami Aras Kubilay, AvMP</a>, our Business Development Director and <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/onuryilmaz67?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Onur YILMAZ</a>, IT Consultant at Pegasus Airlines, will share insights into our groundbreaking collaboration.

Discover how we defied conventional approaches in launching our Offers and Orders platform, setting new standards in airline retailing.

✈️

Hitit Oxygen ile Pegasus’a Yeni Bir Nefes  
 
Bugün, 15:45 - 16:00 (GMT+1) saatleri arasında T2RL Engage 2025 – Grand Hall, Track One’de gerçekleşecek değerli sunumda, İş Geliştirme Direktörümüz Aras Kubilay ve Pegasus Havayolları Bilgi Teknolojileri Danışmanı Onur Yılmaz, alışılmış yaklaşımları geride bırakarak, sektördeki mevcut en büyük Teklif ve Sipariş platformunu hayata geçirişimizi ve havayolu perakendeciliğinde yeni standartları nasıl belirlediğimizi paylaşacaklar. 
 
Bu öncü iş birliği ile havayolu perakendeciliğinde yeni bir dönemin kapılarını aralıyoruz. 

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Ft2rlengage2025&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#T2RLEngage2025</a></p>

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">A Productive Day at <a class="link" href="https://uk.linkedin.com/company/t2rl?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>T2RL</a> Engage 2025!
 
As part of the Payment Sessions, our Deputy Director of Payment Solutions, <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/hocalan?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Cagdas Ocalan</a>, shared his insights on integrating secure and efficient payment processes. He joined <a class="link" href="https://ie.linkedin.com/in/jonathan-rockett-34499526?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Jonathan Rockett</a> (<a class="link" href="https://ie.linkedin.com/company/datalex?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Datalex</a>), <a class="link" href="https://uk.linkedin.com/in/esperanza-fernandez-6314b11?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Esperanza Fernandez</a> (<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/mastercard?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Mastercard</a>), <a class="link" href="https://uk.linkedin.com/in/sandra-mianda?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Sandra M.</a> (<a class="link" href="https://uk.linkedin.com/company/paypr-work?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Paypr.work [ˈpeɪpəwəːk]</a>), and <a class="link" href="https://ch.linkedin.com/in/myriam-burget-968739?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Myriam Burget</a> (<a class="link" href="https://ch.linkedin.com/company/swiss-international-air-lines?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Swiss International Air Lines</a>) on stage to discuss the future of payment systems as the industry transitions from PNRs and tickets to retail-style orders. 

If you would like to learn more about payment integrations in aviation and Hitit’s vision in this field, don’t miss the chance to connect with Cagdas at the T2RL Engage Gala Dinner.

***

Ödeme Oturumları kapsamında, İş Geliştirme – Ödeme Hizmetleri Direktörümüz Çağdaş Öcalan, güvenli ve etkili ödeme süreçlerinin entegrasyonuna dair görüşlerini paylaştı. Çağdaş, Datalex’ten Jonathan Rockett, Mastercard’dan Esperanza Fernandez, Payprwork’ten Sandra Mianda ve Swiss International Airlines’tan Myriam Burget ile aynı sahneyi paylaşarak, sektörün PNR ve biletlerden perakende tarzı siparişlere geçiş sürecinde ödeme sistemlerinin geleceğini tartıştı. 

Havacılıkta ödeme entegrasyonları ve Hitit’in bu alandaki vizyonu hakkında daha fazla bilgi almak isteyenler, T2RL Engage Gala Yemeği’nde Çağdaş ile tanışabilir.</p>

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Here’s a glimpse of our team at <a class="link" href="https://uk.linkedin.com/company/t2rl?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>T2RL</a> Engage 2025
 
We are excited to connect with so many valuable industry peers at Convene, St. Paul’s, London. 

Our CEO <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/nevra-onursal-karaagac-742168?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Nevra Onursal Karaagac</a>, Sales Director <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/cem-k%C4%B1rg%C4%B1z-4b718110?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Cem Kırgız</a>, Business Development Director <a class="link" href="https://nl.linkedin.com/in/araskubilay?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Sami Aras Kubilay, AvMP</a>, and Deputy Director of Payment Solutions <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/hocalan?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Cagdas Ocalan</a> are looking forward to catching up with fellow professionals, meeting you, and sharing Hitit’s recent groundbreaking innovations.

Over the next few days, we will be sharing insights and perspectives on the future of airline retailing and payments.

Keep an eye out for highlights from our sessions and activities at the conference.
 
✈️ ✈️ 

T2RL Engage 2025’te Hitit ekibi olarak bir aradayız 

Londra, St. Paul’s Convene’de değerli sektör paydaşlarımızla buluşuyoruz. 
Genel Müdürümüz Nevra Onursal Karaağaç, Satış Direktörümüz Cem Kırgız, İş Geliştirme Direktörümüz Aras Kubilay ve İş Geliştirme – Ödeme Hizmetleri Direktörümüz Çağdaş Öcalan, sektörün diğer profesyonelleriyle buluşmayı ve Hitit’in son dönemde sektörde çığır açan yeniliklerini paylaşmayı sabırsızlıkla bekliyor. 

Önümüzdeki günlerde de havacılık perakendeciliği ve ödemelerin geleceğine dair görüş ve deneyimlerimizi paylaşacağız. 

Etkinlik süresince katılacağımız panel ve sunumlarımıza dair paylaşımlarımızı kaçırmayın. 

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Ft2rlengage2025&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#T2RLEngage2025</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fhitit&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Hitit</a></p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Future of Airline Payments

The shift from PNRs and tickets to retail-style Orders is transforming aviation, but without effective payment management, this move to Offer, Order, Settle, and Delivery (OOSD) cannot happen.

Today, from 14:15 to 14:55 at the Payments Track, our Deputy Director of Payment Solutions - <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/hocalan?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Cagdas Ocalan</a>, will take the stage for the panel “Bring the Money In or Nothing Else Matters”, sharing insights on achieving secure and efficient settlement across the entire value chain.

✈️

Havacılıkta Ödemelerin Geleceği

PNR’lardan ve biletlerden perakendecilik yaklaşımı ile kurgulanmış Sipariş modeline geçiş, havacılığı dönüştürüyor; ancak bu geçişin Teklif, Sipariş, Mutabakat ve Teslimat (Offer, Order, Settle, and Delivery – OOSD) modelinde başarılı olabilmesi için etkili ödeme yönetimi şart.

Bugün, 14:15 – 14:55 arasında Ödeme Oturumları kapsamında, İş Geliştirme – Ödeme Hizmetleri Direktörümüz Çağdaş Öcalan sahnede olacak ve tüm değer zincirinde güvenli ve etkili ödeme süreçlerinin nasıl entegre edilebileceğine dair görüşlerini paylaşacak.

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Foosd&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#OOSD</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Faviation&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Aviation</a></p>

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">The IATA Cargo Experts Conference 2025 will take place in Brussels from 24–25 September, gathering industry leaders to discuss the future of air cargo with a focus on digitalization, innovation, and operational excellence.

Hitit will be represented by our Cargo team —<a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/atilla-lise-22943510?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Atilla Lise</a>, <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/murat-gurdogan?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Murat Gurdogan</a>, and Can Okcabollu — who will join peers from across the industry to exchange insights and shape the next era of cargo. 

As part of the conference, our Chief Transportation Solutions Officer, Mr. Atilla Lise, will speak at the panel “Industry Readiness for ONE Record 1-1-2026: Where Do We Stand” on Wednesday, 24 September, 11:45–12:30. The session will explore how the industry is preparing for this important milestone and its impact on cargo operations worldwide.

Later the same day, from 14:20–14:40, Murat Gürdoğan and Can Okcabollu will deliver a joint presentation in the ONE Record Use Cases session, titled:
“One API to File Them All: PLACI Customs with ONE Record.”

We look forward to contributing to the conversation on building a more connected and efficient cargo ecosystem.

✈️ ✈️ 

Hitit olarak 24–25 Eylül tarihlerinde Brüksel’de gerçekleşecek IATA Cargo Experts Conference 2025’te hava kargo dünyasının liderleri ile bir araya geleceğiz. 

Ulaştırma Çözümlerinden Sorumlu Genel Müdür Yardımcımız Atilla Lise, 24 Eylül Çarşamba 11:45–12:30 arasında “ONE Record 1-1-2026’a Hazırlıkta Sektör Nerede?” konulu panelde sahne alacak ve ONE Record’a geçiş hazırlıkları ile sektörün güncel durumu üzerine görüşlerini paylaşacak. 

Aynı gün 14:20–14:40 saatleri arasında ise Murat Gürdoğan ve Can Okcabollu, ONE Record Use Cases oturumunda “Hepsi için Tek Bir API: ONE Record ile PLACI Gümrükleri” başlıklı ortak sunumlarını gerçekleştirecekler. 

Hava kargonun geleceğini konuşmak ve fikir alışverişinde bulunmak üzere bu değerli platformda yer almaktan memnuniyet duyuyoruz.
